### [36] [The Moral Consistency Pipeline: Continuous Ethical Evaluation for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03026)
*Saeid Jamshidi,Kawser Wazed Nafi,Arghavan Moradi Dakhel,Negar Shahabi,Foutse Khomh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个名为MoCoP的无需数据集的闭环框架，用于持续评估和解释大型语言模型（LLMs）的道德稳定性。MoCoP通过词汇完整性分析、语义风险估计和基于推理的判断建模，能够自主生成、评估和优化伦理场景。实验表明，MoCoP能有效捕捉LLMs的长期道德行为，揭示了道德与毒性维度之间存在强烈的负相关（rET = -0.81），而与响应延迟几乎没有关联（rEL ≈ 0）。研究结论是，道德一致性和语言安全性是模型行为中稳定且可解释的特征，而非短期波动。MoCoP为可扩展、连续的审计提供了一个可复现的基础，并推动了自主AI系统中计算道德的研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型（LLMs）对齐框架通常依赖于静态数据集和事后评估，难以揭示模型在不同情境和时间尺度下道德推理的演变。这导致在模型快速发展和适应能力增强的背景下，对其道德一致性（在不同情境下保持伦理连贯推理的能力）的评估存在局限性。因此，有必要开发一种能够持续评估和解释LLMs道德稳定性的新方法。

Method: 该研究提出了一种名为MoCoP（Moral Consistency Pipeline）的无需数据集、闭环框架。MoCoP包含三个支撑层：词汇完整性分析、语义风险估计和基于推理的判断建模。该框架在一个自给自足的架构中运行，能够自主地生成、评估和优化伦理场景，而无需外部监督。在GPT-4-Turbo和DeepSeek模型上进行了实证评估。

Result: 实证结果表明，MoCoP能够有效地捕捉LLMs的长期道德行为。研究发现，道德维度和毒性维度之间存在显著的负相关关系（相关系数rET = -0.81，p值小于0.001），而道德一致性与响应延迟之间几乎没有关联（相关系数rEL约等于0）。这表明模型的道德一致性和语言安全性是稳定且可解释的特征，而非短期内的波动。

Conclusion: MoCoP框架通过将伦理评估重新定义为一种动态的、与模型无关的道德内省形式，为可扩展、连续的审计提供了可复现的基础。研究结果证实，道德一致性是LLMs的一种稳定且可解释的特性，并为未来在自主AI系统中研究计算道德提供了新的方向。该研究强调了持续监控和评估LLMs道德行为的重要性。

Abstract: The rapid advancement and adaptability of Large Language Models (LLMs) highlight the need for moral consistency, the capacity to maintain ethically coherent reasoning across varied contexts. Existing alignment frameworks, structured approaches designed to align model behavior with human ethical and social norms, often rely on static datasets and post-hoc evaluations, offering limited insight into how ethical reasoning may evolve across different contexts or temporal scales. This study presents the Moral Consistency Pipeline (MoCoP), a dataset-free, closed-loop framework for continuously evaluating and interpreting the moral stability of LLMs. MoCoP combines three supporting layers: (i) lexical integrity analysis, (ii) semantic risk estimation, and (iii) reasoning-based judgment modeling within a self-sustaining architecture that autonomously generates, evaluates, and refines ethical scenarios without external supervision. Our empirical results on GPT-4-Turbo and DeepSeek suggest that MoCoP effectively captures longitudinal ethical behavior, revealing a strong inverse relationship between ethical and toxicity dimensions (correlation rET = -0.81, p value less than 0.001) and a near-zero association with response latency (correlation rEL approximately equal to 0). These findings demonstrate that moral coherence and linguistic safety tend to emerge as stable and interpretable characteristics of model behavior rather than short-term fluctuations. Furthermore, by reframing ethical evaluation as a dynamic, model-agnostic form of moral introspection, MoCoP offers a reproducible foundation for scalable, continuous auditing and advances the study of computational morality in autonomous AI systems.

</details>


### [37] [On SkipGram Word Embedding Models with Negative Sampling: Unified Framework and Impact of Noise Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2009.04413)
*Dezhi Liu,Richong Zhang,Ziqiao Wang*

Method: 本文提出了一种名为词-上下文分类（WCC）的框架，该框架通过引入“噪声样本”来概括SGN模型。通过理论分析证明了引入噪声样本的合理性，并实验研究了噪声分布对WCC嵌入模型学习的影响，比较了不同噪声分布下的嵌入性能和收敛速度。

Abstract: SkipGram word embedding models with negative sampling, or SGN in short, is an elegant family of word embedding models. In this paper, we formulate a framework for word embedding, referred to as Word-Context Classification (WCC), that generalizes SGN to a wide family of models. The framework, which uses some ``noise examples'', is justified through theoretical analysis. The impact of noise distribution on the learning of the WCC embedding models is studied experimentally, suggesting that the best noise distribution is, in fact, the data distribution, in terms of both the embedding performance and the speed of convergence during training. Along our way, we discover several novel embedding models that outperform existing WCC models.

Abstract: Word embeddings and language models have transformed natural language processing (NLP) by facilitating the representation of linguistic elements in continuous vector spaces. This review visits foundational concepts such as the distributional hypothesis and contextual similarity, tracing the evolution from sparse representations like one-hot encoding to dense embeddings including Word2Vec, GloVe, and fastText. By synthesizing current methodologies and emerging trends, this survey offers researchers and practitioners an in-depth resource to push the boundaries of embedding-based language models.

### [39] [SkyLadder: Better and Faster Pretraining via Context Window Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2503.15450)
*Tongyao Zhu,Qian Liu,Haonan Wang,Shiqi Chen,Xiangming Gu,Tianyu Pang,Min-Yen Kan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 在固定 token 预算下，具有较短上下文窗口预训练的模型在长上下文任务上优于其长上下文对应物。为解决此问题，本文提出了 SkyLadder，一种从短到长上下文窗口的过渡策略，该策略在保持标准基准性能的同时，提高了长上下文任务的效率和效果。实验证明 SkyLadder 可在常见基准上带来高达 3.7% 的性能提升，并使训练速度提高 22%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型（LLM）在预训练中不断扩展上下文窗口以处理更长序列，但一项初步研究发现，在固定 token 预算下，使用较短上下文窗口预训练的模型在长上下文任务上的表现却优于其长上下文的对应模型。这种现象表明，在上下文窗口长度和预训练效率之间可能存在一个权衡，这促使研究人员探索一种能够更好地平衡两者的新策略。

Method: 本文提出了 SkyLadder，一种简单而有效的策略，通过实现从短到长上下文窗口的过渡来实现。该方法旨在优化预训练过程，通过逐步增加上下文窗口的长度来训练模型。实验中，研究人员在 100B tokens 上预训练了参数量为 1B（上下文长度高达 32K）和 3B（上下文长度 8K）的模型，并将 SkyLadder 的性能与基线方法进行了比较。

Result: SkyLadder 在标准基准测试中保持了强大的性能，并且在长上下文任务上达到了与基线相当甚至更好的结果。具体而言，与基线方法相比，SkyLadder 在常见基准测试中带来了高达 3.7% 的一致性性能提升，同时训练速度最高可提高 22%。

Conclusion: SkyLadder 是一种有效的上下文窗口调度策略，它成功地平衡了长上下文能力和预训练效率。该方法在不牺牲标准性能的情况下，提高了模型在长上下文任务上的表现，并显著加快了训练速度。研究结果表明，通过优化上下文窗口的训练策略，可以更有效地提升 LLM 的性能。未来研究可进一步探索更复杂的调度策略或将其应用于更大规模的模型。代码已开源。

Abstract: Recent advancements in LLM pretraining have featured ever-expanding context windows to process longer sequences. However, our pilot study reveals that models pretrained with shorter context windows consistently outperform their long-context counterparts under a fixed token budget. This finding motivates us to explore an optimal context window scheduling strategy to better balance long-context capability with pretraining efficiency. To this end, we propose SkyLadder, a simple yet effective approach that implements a short-to-long context window transition. SkyLadder preserves strong standard benchmark performance, while matching or exceeding baseline results on long context tasks. Through extensive experiments, we pre-train 1B-parameter models (up to 32K context) and 3B-parameter models (8K context) on 100B tokens, demonstrating that SkyLadder yields consistent gains of up to 3.7% on common benchmarks, while achieving up to 22% faster training speeds compared to baselines. The code is at https://github.com/sail-sg/SkyLadder.

### [40] [Induction Head Toxicity Mechanistically Explains Repetition Curse in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.13514)
*Shuxun Wang,Qingyu Yin,Chak Tou Leong,Qiang Zhang,Linyi Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型语言模型（LLMs）中“重复诅咒”现象的诱因，发现与归纳头（induction heads）的“毒性”——即在生成过程中主导输出的趋势——密切相关。研究提出了通过注意力头正则化来减轻归纳头主导地位，从而减少重复现象的技术，并为LLMs的设计和训练提供了新的视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在生成文本时，常常会陷入“重复诅咒”的现象，即生成重复或循环的序列。尽管这一现象普遍存在，但其根本原因尚不明确。理解并解决重复诅咒对于提升LLMs的生成质量至关重要。

Method: 本研究深入探究了注意力机制中的“归纳头”在驱动重复行为中的作用。研究者定义了归纳头的“毒性”，即它们在重复生成过程中主导模型输出的概率（logits）并排斥其他注意力头贡献的倾向。在此基础上，提出了一种结合注意力头正则化的技术，旨在降低归纳头在生成过程中的主导性。

Result: 研究发现，归纳头的“毒性”是导致LLMs重复诅咒的关键因素。通过实验证明，归纳头确实倾向于在重复序列生成时占据主导地位。提出的注意力头正则化技术能够有效降低归纳头的主导性，从而促进模型生成更多样化和连贯的文本。

Conclusion: 本文通过识别归纳头在重复诅咒中的核心作用，为这一现象提供了力所能及的机制性解释。研究提出的注意力头正则化技术为减轻重复现象提供了潜在的解决方案，对于未来LLMs的设计和训练具有重要的指导意义。未来的工作可以进一步探索正则化技术的优化和在不同模型架构上的应用。

Abstract: Repetition curse is a phenomenon where Large Language Models (LLMs) generate repetitive sequences of tokens or cyclic sequences. While the repetition curse has been widely observed, its underlying mechanisms remain poorly understood. In this work, we investigate the role of induction heads--a specific type of attention head known for their ability to perform in-context learning--in driving this repetitive behavior. Specifically, we focus on the "toxicity" of induction heads, which we define as their tendency to dominate the model's output logits during repetition, effectively excluding other attention heads from contributing to the generation process. Our findings have important implications for the design and training of LLMs. By identifying induction heads as a key driver of the repetition curse, we provide a mechanistic explanation for this phenomenon and suggest potential avenues for mitigation. We also propose a technique with attention head regularization that could be employed to reduce the dominance of induction heads during generation, thereby promoting more diverse and coherent outputs.

### [41] [ELSPR: Evaluator LLM Training Data Self-Purification on Non-Transitive Preferences via Tournament Graph Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.17691)
*Yan Yu,Yilun Liu,Minggui He,Shimin Tao,Weibin Meng,Xinhua Yang,Li Zhang,Hongxia Ma,Dengye Li,Daimeng Wei,Boxing Chen,Fuliang Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Pairwise evaluation of LLMs is undermined by non-transitive preferences due to low-quality data. ELSPR, a graph-theoretic framework, identifies and filters problematic data by modeling preferences as tournament graphs and using SCC analysis and a novel entropy metric. Experiments on AlpacaEval show ELSPR-filtered data significantly reduces non-transitivity and improves model performance, with human validation confirming lower agreement on discarded data. ELSPR offers an effective data self-purification method for robust LLM evaluation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Pairwise evaluation is dominant for LLM benchmarking on open-ended tasks, but non-transitive preferences (A>B, B>C, C>A) compromise ranking reliability. This issue often stems from ambiguous preference data. Addressing this is crucial for developing dependable LLM evaluation systems.

Method: ELSPR, a graph-theoretic framework, models pairwise LLM preferences as tournament graphs. It uses strongly connected components (SCCs) analysis to quantify non-transitivity and a novel normalized directed graph structural entropy metric to measure preference clarity. A filtering methodology is employed to remove data inducing non-transitivity while retaining transitive preferences. The approach was tested on the AlpacaEval benchmark.

Result: Models fine-tuned on ELSPR-filtered data showed significant improvements: a 13.8% reduction in non-transitivity, a 0.088 decrease in structural entropy, and enhanced discriminative power in evaluation systems. Human validation revealed substantially lower inter-annotator agreement (34.4% vs. 52.6%) and model-human consistency (51.2% vs. 80.6%) for discarded data compared to cleaned data.

Conclusion: ELSPR is an effective data self-purification approach for LLM evaluation. By systematically identifying and filtering low-quality, non-transitive preference data using graph theory, it leads to more robust, consistent, and human-aligned LLM evaluation systems. Future work could explore extending ELSPR to other benchmarking paradigms or incorporating more sophisticated graph-based metrics.

Abstract: Pairwise evaluation of large language models (LLMs) has become the dominant paradigm for benchmarking open-ended tasks, yet non-transitive preferences, where evaluators prefer A over B, B over C, but C over A, fundamentally undermine ranking reliability. We show that this critical issue stems largely from low-quality data that contains inherently ambiguous preference pairs. To address this challenge, we propose ELSPR, a principled graph-theoretic framework that models pairwise preferences as tournament graphs and systematically identifies problematic training data. ELSPR quantifies non-transitivity through strongly connected components (SCCs) analysis and measures overall preference clarity using a novel normalized directed graph structural entropy metric. Our filtering methodology selectively removes preference data that induce non-transitivity while preserving transitive preferences. Extensive experiments on the AlpacaEval benchmark demonstrate that models fine-tuned on ELSPR-filtered data achieve substantial improvements: a 13.8% reduction in non-transitivity, a 0.088 decrease in structural entropy, and significantly enhanced discriminative power in real-world evaluation systems. Human validation confirms that discarded data exhibit dramatically lower inter-annotator agreement (34.4% vs. 52.6%) and model-human consistency (51.2% vs. 80.6%) compared to cleaned data. These findings establish ELSPR as an effective data self-purification approach for developing more robust, consistent, and human-aligned LLM evaluation systems.

</details>


### [42] [Multilingual Pretraining for Pixel Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2505.21265)
*Ilker Kesen,Jonas F. Lotz,Ingo Ziegler,Phillip Rust,Desmond Elliott*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Pixel language models (PIXEL) process images of text directly, bypassing fixed vocabularies and showing strong cross-lingual transfer. This paper introduces PIXEL-M4, pretrained on English, Hindi, Ukrainian, and Simplified Chinese. PIXEL-M4 surpasses English-only models on non-Latin scripts and demonstrates robust linguistic feature capture, even in unseen languages. Its multilingual pretraining leads to aligned semantic embedding spaces across languages, proving its effectiveness for diverse language support.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional language models rely on fixed vocabularies, limiting their ability to handle diverse languages and scripts, especially those not well-represented in large text corpora. Pixel language models offer a promising alternative by operating directly on image representations of text, thus inherently supporting any script. However, the potential of multilingual pretraining for these pixel-based models, especially across visually and linguistically diverse languages, remains largely unexplored. This research addresses this gap by investigating whether multilingual pretraining can enhance the performance and linguistic understanding of pixel language models across a broader range of languages, particularly those with non-Latin scripts.

Method: The researchers developed PIXEL-M4, a pixel language model pretrained on a diverse multilingual dataset. This dataset included four languages: English (Latin script), Hindi (Devanagari script), Ukrainian (Cyrillic script), and Simplified Chinese (Hanzi script). The pretraining aimed to expose the model to different visual and linguistic characteristics. After pretraining, PIXEL-M4 was evaluated on various downstream tasks, including semantic and syntactic evaluations. To further understand the model's capabilities, word-level probing analyses were conducted to assess its ability to capture linguistic features. Additionally, an analysis of the model's hidden representations was performed to examine the alignment of semantic embedding spaces across the pretraining languages.

Result: Multilingual evaluations demonstrated that PIXEL-M4 significantly outperformed an English-only pixel language model baseline, particularly on tasks involving non-Latin scripts. The word-level probing analyses confirmed that PIXEL-M4 effectively captures rich linguistic features, extending to languages that were not part of its pretraining set. The analysis of hidden representations revealed that multilingual pretraining resulted in a semantic embedding space that was closely aligned across English, Hindi, Ukrainian, and Simplified Chinese. This suggests a shared underlying semantic understanding developed through the multilingual pretraining process.

Conclusion: This work successfully demonstrates that multilingual pretraining is a highly effective strategy for enhancing the capabilities of pixel language models. By pretraining PIXEL-M4 on a diverse set of four languages, the model achieved superior performance on non-Latin scripts and showed improved linguistic feature representation. The aligned semantic embedding space across languages highlights the model's ability to generalize and understand semantic concepts universally. This research validates the approach of using pixel-based models with multilingual pretraining as a powerful method for supporting a wide array of languages, paving the way for more inclusive and versatile language technologies.

Abstract: Pixel language models operate directly on images of rendered text, eliminating the need for a fixed vocabulary. While these models have demonstrated strong capabilities for downstream cross-lingual transfer, multilingual pretraining remains underexplored. We introduce PIXEL-M4, a model pretrained on four visually and linguistically diverse languages: English, Hindi, Ukrainian, and Simplified Chinese. Multilingual evaluations on semantic and syntactic tasks show that PIXEL-M4 outperforms an English-only counterpart on non-Latin scripts. Word-level probing analyses confirm that PIXEL-M4 captures rich linguistic features, even in languages not seen during pretraining. Furthermore, an analysis of its hidden representations shows that multilingual pretraining yields a semantic embedding space closely aligned across the languages used for pretraining. This work demonstrates that multilingual pretraining substantially enhances the capability of pixel language models to effectively support a diverse set of languages.

### [43] [Eka-Eval: An Evaluation Framework for Low-Resource Multilingual Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.01853)
*Samridhi Raj Sinha,Rajvee Sheth,Abhishek Upperwal,Mayank Singh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: EKA-EVAL是一个统一的、端到端的评估框架，旨在解决大型语言模型评估的挑战。它提供了广泛的语言支持、模型类型和任务，具有零代码Web界面和交互式CLI，易于访问。该框架集成了50多个多语言基准，支持本地和专有模型，并提供11项核心功能。与现有基线相比，EKA-EVAL在可用性、用户满意度、设置时间和基准可重复性方面均有显著改进，是首个提供全面覆盖的单一平台。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: EKA-EVAL框架采用统一的、端到端的架构，结合了零代码Web界面和交互式命令行界面（CLI），以实现广泛的可访问性。它集成了50多个多语言基准，涵盖九个评估类别，并支持本地和专有模型。该框架具有模块化、即插即用的特性，提供了11项核心功能，支持可扩展的多语言评估，特别关注低资源语言。

Result: 与五个现有基线相比，EKA-EVAL在关键可用性指标上至少提高了2倍。用户满意度最高，设置时间更快，并且基准可重复性得到保证。

Conclusion: EKA-EVAL是一个创新的一站式评估平台，为LLM的多语言、大规模评估提供了解决方案。它通过提高可用性、用户满意度和效率，显著优于现有方法。该框架的开源性质及其对低资源语言的支持，将进一步推动LLM研究和应用的普及。未来的工作可以继续扩展基准库，并探索更先进的评估指标。

Abstract: The rapid evolution of Large Language Models' has underscored the need for evaluation frameworks that are globally applicable, flexible, and modular, and that support a wide range of tasks, model types, and linguistic settings. We introduce EKA-EVAL, a unified, end- to-end framework that combines a zero-code web interface and an interactive CLI to ensure broad accessibility. It integrates 50+ multilingual benchmarks across nine evaluation categories, supports local and proprietary models, and provides 11 core capabilities through a modular, plug-and-play architecture. Designed for scalable, multilingual evaluation with support for low-resource multilingual languages, EKA-EVAL is, to the best of our knowledge, the first suite to offer comprehensive coverage in a single platform. Comparisons against five existing baselines indicate improvements of at least 2x better on key usability measures, with the highest user satisfaction, faster setup times, and consistent benchmark reproducibility. The framework is open-source and publicly available at https://github.com/lingo-iitgn/eka-eval.

### [44] [LLMEval-3: A Large-Scale Longitudinal Study on Robust and Fair Evaluation of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.05452)
*Ming Zhang,Yujiong Shen,Jingyi Deng,Yuhui Wang,Yue Zhang,Junzhe Wang,Shichun Liu,Shihan Dou,Huayu Sha,Qiyuan Peng,Changhao Jiang,Jingqi Tong,Yilong Wu,Zhihao Zhang,Mingqi Wu,Zhiheng Xi,Mingxu Chai,Tao Gui,Qi Zhang,Xuanjing Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LLMEval-3是一个动态评估框架，使用专有的220k研究生级别问题库，通过动态采样创建未见过的测试集，以解决现有LLM静态基准测试中的数据污染和排行榜过拟合问题。该框架通过数据自动管理、抗作弊机制和与人类专家有90%一致性的LLM-as-a-judge流程，以及相对排名系统，确保了评估的完整性和公平性。长达20个月的研究表明，LLMEval-3能揭示静态基准测试无法检测到的性能瓶颈和数据污染漏洞，并提供了稳定的模型排名，证明了动态评估的有效性，有助于建立更可信的LLM评估标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型（LLM）评估方法依赖于静态基准测试，这些测试容易受到数据污染和排行榜过度拟合的影响。这意味着评估结果可能无法真实反映模型的实际能力，阻碍了对LLM真实水平的准确衡量，并可能误导模型的发展方向。因此，迫切需要一种更可靠、更能抵抗污染的评估方法。

Method: LLMEval-3框架通过以下方式实现动态评估：1. 专有题库：构建了一个包含22万个研究生级别问题的题库。2. 动态采样：每次评估运行时，从题库中动态抽取未见过的测试集，确保模型无法预先接触到测试数据。3. 自动化流程：包括抗污染的数据整理、创新的反作弊架构以及一个与人类专家有90%一致性的校准LLM-as-a-judge流程。4. 相对排名系统：用于模型之间的公平比较。5. 长期研究：进行了为期20个月的实验，评估了近50个领先模型。

Result: LLMEval-3在长达20个月的评估中，揭示了模型在知识记忆方面存在性能瓶颈，并暴露了静态基准测试无法检测到的数据污染漏洞。该框架在排名稳定性和一致性方面表现出卓越的鲁棒性，为动态评估范式提供了强有力的实证支持。与人类专家的比较显示，LLM-as-a-judge流程具有很高的准确性。

Conclusion: LLMEval-3提供了一种比静态排行榜分数更可靠、更可信的方法来评估LLM的真实能力。它通过动态采样和抗污染机制，有效解决了数据污染和排行榜过度拟合的问题，为LLM评估树立了新的、更严格的标准，推动了更值得信赖的评估体系的发展。未来的工作可以进一步扩展题库规模和多样性，并探索更复杂的评估维度。

Abstract: Existing evaluation of Large Language Models (LLMs) on static benchmarks is vulnerable to data contamination and leaderboard overfitting, critical issues that obscure true model capabilities. To address this, we introduce LLMEval-3, a framework for dynamic evaluation of LLMs. LLMEval-3 is built on a proprietary bank of 220k graduate-level questions, from which it dynamically samples unseen test sets for each evaluation run. Its automated pipeline ensures integrity via contamination-resistant data curation, a novel anti-cheating architecture, and a calibrated LLM-as-a-judge process achieving 90% agreement with human experts, complemented by a relative ranking system for fair comparison. An 20-month longitudinal study of nearly 50 leading models reveals a performance ceiling on knowledge memorization and exposes data contamination vulnerabilities undetectable by static benchmarks. The framework demonstrates exceptional robustness in ranking stability and consistency, providing strong empirical validation for the dynamic evaluation paradigm. LLMEval-3 offers a robust and credible methodology for assessing the true capabilities of LLMs beyond leaderboard scores, promoting the development of more trustworthy evaluation standards.

### [45] [Just-in-time and distributed task representations in language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.04466)
*Yuxuan Li,Declan Campbell,Stephanie C. Y. Chan,Andrew Kyle Lampinen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了语言模型在上下文中学习新任务时，任务表示的形成和演变过程。研究发现，可迁移的任务表示（transferrable task representations）以非单调和零星的方式演变，表现出“时序局部性”（temporal locality），仅在特定 token 处出现，并且能随着更多示例的提供而累积证据。同时，任务身份表示（task identity representations）在整个上下文中保持稳定。部分可迁移表示还表现出“语义局部性”（semantic locality），仅限于特定子任务。最终，语言模型通过持续的任务敏感性和即时生成的表示来动态地学习新任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型在没有权重更新的情况下，仅通过上下文（指令或示例）就能学习新任务的能力（即上下文学习）是其强大功能的重要来源。然而，对于这些新任务的表示何时在模型内部形成，以及它们如何在上下文的演变过程中发生变化，我们知之甚少。理解这一点对于揭示语言模型的内部工作机制、提高其学习效率和可控性至关重要。

Method: 本研究通过分析两种不同的任务表示：一种是“可迁移表示”（transferrable representations），即即使没有完整的提示也能迁移到另一个模型实例的向量表示；另一种是更高层次的任务类别表示。研究者们追踪这些表示在模型处理上下文信息时随时间（token 序列）的变化，特别关注其形成的时机、对示例数量的响应以及其影响的范围（局部性）。

Result: 研究结果表明，可迁移的任务表示演变方式具有非单调性和零星性，并且表现出“时序局部性”：它们仅在序列中的特定 token 处出现，尽管任务身份信息在整个上下文中都能被可靠地解码。当提供更多示例时，可迁移表示能够有效地整合证据，体现出“证据累积”的特点。此外，部分可迁移表示还表现出“语义局部性”，即仅限于一个较小的任务范围，例如一个独立的子任务。相比之下，任务身份表示在整个上下文中都保持稳定。

Conclusion: 语言模型并非以单一、静态的方式来表示新任务。相反，它们通过两种机制动态地学习和表示新任务：一种是持续存在的、对任务保持敏感的“惰性”表示（即任务身份表示）；另一种是为支持推理而“适时”生成的“主动”表示（即可迁移任务表示）。这种“即时生成”和“惰性”表示的结合，使得语言模型能够灵活有效地适应新任务。未来的研究可以进一步探索这些表示的神经机制，以及如何更精确地控制和利用它们。

Abstract: Many of language models' impressive capabilities originate from their in-context learning: based on instructions or examples, they can infer and perform new tasks without weight updates. In this work, we investigate when representations for new tasks are formed in language models, and how these representations change over the course of context. We study two different task representations: those that are ''transferrable'' -- vector representations that can transfer task contexts to another model instance, even without the full prompt -- and simpler representations of high-level task categories. We show that transferrable task representations evolve in non-monotonic and sporadic ways, while task identity representations persist throughout the context. Specifically, transferrable task representations exhibit a two-fold locality. They successfully condense evidence when more examples are provided in the context. But this evidence accrual process exhibits strong temporal locality along the sequence dimension, coming online only at certain tokens -- despite task identity being reliably decodable throughout the context. In some cases, transferrable task representations also show semantic locality, capturing a small task ''scope'' such as an independent subtask. Language models thus represent new tasks on the fly through both an inert, sustained sensitivity to the task and an active, just-in-time representation to support inference.

</details>


### [46] [Evolution and compression in LLMs: On the emergence of human-aligned categorization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.08093)
*Nathaniel Imel,Noga Zaslavsky*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）是否能像人类一样，通过信息瓶颈（IB）原理形成高效的语义类别系统，特别是以颜色分类为例。研究发现，指令微调的LLMs在颜色命名方面表现出不同程度的复杂性和与人类的对齐程度，其中更大的模型表现更好。通过模拟文化演化过程（IICLL），研究证明LLMs能够像人类一样，将随机的颜色命名系统迭代地重构为更符合IB原理的系统。然而，只有能力最强的模型（Gemini 2.0）能够重现人类观察到的近乎最优的IB权衡范围，而其他模型则收敛于低复杂度解。这表明LLMs可以通过与人类相同的基本原理发展出人类对齐的语义类别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类的语义类别系统在信息压缩方面接近最优，遵循信息瓶颈（IB）的复杂性-准确性权衡。然而，大型语言模型（LLMs）的训练目标并非如此，这引发了一个关键问题：LLMs是否能够自主发展出与人类一致的高效语义系统？理解这一点对于评估LLMs的认知能力、发展更符合人类心智的模型以及探索语言和认知的进化机制至关重要。本研究选择颜色分类作为核心研究对象，因为它在认知理论中是分类研究的重要领域，并且拥有丰富的人类数据可供借鉴和比较。

Method: 本研究采用了两步实验方法。首先，研究人员在一项针对颜色的命名研究中，复现了两个有影响力的、针对人类的认知实验。他们使用LLMs进行英文颜色命名，并分析模型的复杂性和与人类语言的对齐程度。其次，为了探究LLMs是仅仅模仿训练数据中的模式，还是真正具备了偏向IB效率的类人归纳偏见，研究人员引入了一种名为“迭代式语境内学习”（IICLL）的方法。通过这种方法，他们模拟了LLMs在伪颜色命名系统中的文化演化过程，观察其如何迭代地调整命名系统。

Result: 在英文颜色命名研究中，结果显示LLMs在复杂性和与人类的对齐程度方面存在显著差异。较大的指令微调模型在颜色命名上表现出更好的对齐性和IB效率。在IICLL模拟的文化演化实验中，研究发现LLMs确实能够像人类一样，将初始随机的颜色命名系统迭代地重构，使其朝着更高的IB效率发展。然而，只有能力最强的模型Gemini 2.0能够重现人类研究中观察到的广泛的、接近最优的IB权衡，而其他先进模型则收敛于复杂度较低的解决方案。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，LLMs有潜力通过与人类相同的基本原理（即信息瓶颈）来发展出人类对齐的语义类别。LLMs能够通过迭代过程优化颜色命名系统，展现出类似人类的归纳偏见。然而，不同模型在实现接近人类最优IB权衡的能力上存在差异，最强大的模型才能完全复现人类的这种能力。这一发现为理解LLMs的语义表征和认知能力提供了新的视角，并指明了未来在模型设计和评估方向上的可能路径。未来的研究可以进一步探索其他语义领域，并深化对不同模型架构和训练策略影响的理解。

Abstract: Converging evidence suggests that human systems of semantic categories achieve near-optimal compression via the Information Bottleneck (IB) complexity-accuracy tradeoff. Large language models (LLMs) are not trained for this objective, which raises the question: are LLMs capable of evolving efficient human-aligned semantic systems? To address this question, we focus on color categorization -- a key testbed of cognitive theories of categorization with uniquely rich human data -- and replicate with LLMs two influential human studies. First, we conduct an English color-naming study, showing that LLMs vary widely in their complexity and English-alignment, with larger instruction-tuned models achieving better alignment and IB-efficiency. Second, to test whether these LLMs simply mimic patterns in their training data or actually exhibit a human-like inductive bias toward IB-efficiency, we simulate cultural evolution of pseudo color-naming systems in LLMs via a method we refer to as Iterated in-Context Language Learning (IICLL). We find that akin to humans, LLMs iteratively restructure initially random systems towards greater IB-efficiency. However, only a model with strongest in-context capabilities (Gemini 2.0) is able to recapitulate the wide range of near-optimal IB-tradeoffs observed in humans, while other state-of-the-art models converge to low-complexity solutions. These findings demonstrate how human-aligned semantic categories can emerge in LLMs via the same fundamental principle that underlies semantic efficiency in humans.

</details>


### [47] [Geometric Uncertainty for Detecting and Correcting Hallucinations in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.13813)
*Edward Phillips,Sean Wu,Soheila Molaei,Danielle Belgrave,Anshul Thakur,David Clifton*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于类比分析的几何框架，用于量化大型语言模型的（不确定性），以检测和减少幻觉。该框架通过计算类比推导的凸包体积（全局不确定性）和响应与类比的空间关系（局部不确定性）来评估响应的可靠性。实验表明，该方法在短期问答和医学数据集上表现优于现有方法，并且证明了凸包体积与熵之间的理论联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）在各种任务中表现出色，但仍存在生成看似合理但事实错误的“幻觉”问题。不确定性量化被认为是检测幻觉的一种策略，但现有方法通常依赖于分散的启发式方法或缺乏统一几何解释的近似图论方法。因此，需要一个统一的几何框架来更有效地进行不确定性量化和幻觉检测。

Method: 研究人员提出了一种基于类比分析的几何框架。该框架首先从批次响应中提取嵌入，然后使用类比分析来识别代表性的“类比”。全局不确定性通过计算由这些类比构成的凸包的体积（几何体积）来衡量。局部不确定性（几何怀疑）通过分析单个响应与其类比的空间关系来评估，从而能够优先选择更可靠的响应以减少幻觉。该方法仅需要对模型进行黑盒访问，并且提供了连续的语义边界点，不同于以往依赖离散成对比较的方法。

Result: 在短期问答数据集上，该框架的表现与现有方法相当或更好。在医学数据集上，该方法取得了更优越的结果，这对于幻觉风险极高的场景尤为重要。此外，研究还通过理论证明了凸包体积与熵之间的联系。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的几何框架为大型语言模型的幻觉检测和不确定性量化提供了一种新颖且有效的解决方案。该方法具有统一的几何解释，并且在多个数据集上都取得了良好的效果，尤其是在对准确性要求极高的医学领域。未来的工作可以进一步探索该框架在更多类型的数据集和任务上的应用，并深化其理论基础。

Abstract: Large language models demonstrate impressive results across diverse tasks but are still known to hallucinate, generating linguistically plausible but incorrect answers to questions. Uncertainty quantification has been proposed as a strategy for hallucination detection, requiring estimates for both global uncertainty (attributed to a batch of responses) and local uncertainty (attributed to individual responses). While recent black-box approaches have shown some success, they often rely on disjoint heuristics or graph-theoretic approximations that lack a unified geometric interpretation. We introduce a geometric framework to address this, based on archetypal analysis of batches of responses sampled with only black-box model access. At the global level, we propose Geometric Volume, which measures the convex hull volume of archetypes derived from response embeddings. At the local level, we propose Geometric Suspicion, which leverages the spatial relationship between responses and these archetypes to rank reliability, enabling hallucination reduction through preferential response selection. Unlike prior methods that rely on discrete pairwise comparisons, our approach provides continuous semantic boundary points which have utility for attributing reliability to individual responses. Experiments show that our framework performs comparably to or better than prior methods on short form question-answering datasets, and achieves superior results on medical datasets where hallucinations carry particularly critical risks. We also provide theoretical justification by proving a link between convex hull volume and entropy.

</details>


### [48] [Apertus: Democratizing Open and Compliant LLMs for Global Language Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.14233)
*Project Apertus,Alejandro Hernández-Cano,Alexander Hägele,Allen Hao Huang,Angelika Romanou,Antoni-Joan Solergibert,Barna Pasztor,Bettina Messmer,Dhia Garbaya,Eduard Frank Ďurech,Ido Hakimi,Juan García Giraldo,Mete Ismayilzada,Negar Foroutan,Skander Moalla,Tiancheng Chen,Vinko Sabolčec,Yixuan Xu,Michael Aerni,Badr AlKhamissi,Inés Altemir Mariñas,Mohammad Hossein Amani,Matin Ansaripour,Ilia Badanin,Harold Benoit,Emanuela Boros,Nicholas Browning,Fabian Bösch,Maximilian Böther,Niklas Canova,Camille Challier,Clement Charmillot,Jonathan Coles,Jan Deriu,Arnout Devos,Lukas Drescher,Daniil Dzenhaliou,Maud Ehrmann,Dongyang Fan,Simin Fan,Silin Gao,Miguel Gila,María Grandury,Diba Hashemi,Alexander Hoyle,Jiaming Jiang,Mark Klein,Andrei Kucharavy,Anastasiia Kucherenko,Frederike Lübeck,Roman Machacek,Theofilos Manitaras,Andreas Marfurt,Kyle Matoba,Simon Matrenok,Henrique Mendonça,Fawzi Roberto Mohamed,Syrielle Montariol,Luca Mouchel,Sven Najem-Meyer,Jingwei Ni,Gennaro Oliva,Matteo Pagliardini,Elia Palme,Andrei Panferov,Léo Paoletti,Marco Passerini,Ivan Pavlov,Auguste Poiroux,Kaustubh Ponkshe,Nathan Ranchin,Javi Rando,Mathieu Sauser,Jakhongir Saydaliev,Muhammad Ali Sayfiddinov,Marian Schneider,Stefano Schuppli,Marco Scialanga,Andrei Semenov,Kumar Shridhar,Raghav Singhal,Anna Sotnikova,Alexander Sternfeld,Ayush Kumar Tarun,Paul Teiletche,Jannis Vamvas,Xiaozhe Yao,Hao Zhao,Alexander Ilic,Ana Klimovic,Andreas Krause,Caglar Gulcehre,David Rosenthal,Elliott Ash,Florian Tramèr,Joost VandeVondele,Livio Veraldi,Martin Rajman,Thomas Schulthess,Torsten Hoefler,Antoine Bosselut,Martin Jaggi,Imanol Schlag*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Apertus是一个完全开放的大型语言模型（LLM）套件，旨在解决当前开放模型生态系统中的数据合规性和多语言表示两大系统性弊端。该模型仅使用公开可用的数据进行预训练，并严格遵守robots.txt排除规则，过滤掉非许可、有毒和包含个人身份信息的内容。为减少信息记忆风险，采用了Goldfish目标函数。Apertus模型还扩展了多语言覆盖范围，涵盖了1800多种语言的15万亿个词元，其中约40%的预训练数据是非英语内容。该模型发布了8B和70B两种规模，在多语言基准测试中，其表现与完全开放模型中的最先进水平相当，甚至超越了部分开放权重模型。此外，还发布了开发过程中的所有科学产物，包括数据准备脚本、检查点、评估套件和训练代码，以实现透明审计和扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当今开放模型生态系统存在数据合规性和多语言表示方面的系统性不足。许多现有模型在发布权重时，缺乏可复现的数据处理流程，且未充分考虑内容所有者的权利。此外，开放模型在多语言能力方面也存在局限性。

Method: Apertus模型仅使用公开可用的数据进行预训练，并严格遵守`robots.txt`协议，过滤有毒、非许可和包含个人身份信息的内容。为降低信息记忆风险，采用了Goldfish目标函数。模型在超过1800种语言的15万亿词元上进行训练，其中约40%为非英语内容。发布了8B和70B两种规模的模型。同时，公开了所有开发过程中的科学产物，包括数据准备脚本、检查点、评估套件和训练代码。

Result: Apertus模型在多语言基准测试中取得了与最先进的完全开放模型相当甚至更优的性能，能够媲美或超越现有的开放权重模型。8B和70B规模的模型均展现出强大的多语言能力。

Conclusion: Apertus通过解决数据合规性和多语言表示问题，为开放大型语言模型生态系统做出了重要贡献。其对数据来源的严格把控、对多语言的广泛支持以及完全开放的科学产物，为后续研究和应用提供了坚实的基础。尽管取得了显著成果，但未来仍可进一步探索更广泛的语言支持和更精细化的数据合规性策略。

Abstract: We present Apertus, a fully open suite of large language models (LLMs) designed to address two systemic shortcomings in today's open model ecosystem: data compliance and multilingual representation. Unlike many prior models that release weights without reproducible data pipelines or regard for content-owner rights, Apertus models are pretrained exclusively on openly available data, retroactively respecting `robots.txt` exclusions and filtering for non-permissive, toxic, and personally identifiable content. To mitigate risks of memorization, we adopt the Goldfish objective during pretraining, strongly suppressing verbatim recall of data while retaining downstream task performance. The Apertus models also expand multilingual coverage, training on 15T tokens from over 1800 languages, with ~40% of pretraining data allocated to non-English content. Released at 8B and 70B scales, Apertus approaches state-of-the-art results among fully open models on multilingual benchmarks, rivalling or surpassing open-weight counterparts. Beyond model weights, we release all scientific artifacts from our development cycle with a permissive license, including data preparation scripts, checkpoints, evaluation suites, and training code, enabling transparent audit and extension.

</details>


### [49] [Look Before you Leap: Estimating LLM Benchmark Scores from Descriptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.20645)
*Jungsoo Park,Ethan Mendes,Gabriel Stanovsky,Alan Ritter*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种在不运行实验的情况下预测大型语言模型（LLM）在特定任务上性能的方法，以解决LLM评估瓶颈问题。研究人员构建了一个名为PRECOG的语料库，包含大量经过处理的任务描述和性能表现配对数据，旨在帮助研究者在早期阶段就预估模型性能，从而更有效地指导实验设计、资源分配和项目决策。实验证明，这种性能预测在一定程度上是可行的，并且即使在零数据泄露的场景下也能取得有意义的预测准确性，为实现“开放式预期评估”迈出了第一步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）的发展面临一个严峻的挑战，即评估瓶颈。传统的评估流程是先构建基准测试，然后运行模型进行测试，最后再根据结果进行迭代改进。这种方法效率低下，耗费大量时间和计算资源。研究人员希望打破这一僵局，探索一种在实验运行之前就能预测模型性能的方法，以便更早地指导研究设计、资源分配和项目优先级排序。例如，开发AI助手的团队可以预估其性能是接近50%还是80%，从而判断是否值得继续投入，以及如何调整项目范围和资源配置。

Method: 研究人员专注于文本任务的性能预测，即模型仅通过分析经过脱敏处理的任务描述和预设配置（不接触任何数据集实例）来预测一个性能分数。为了支持系统性的研究，他们创建了一个名为PRECOG的语料库。该语料库包含了大量脱敏的任务描述-性能表现的配对数据，涵盖了各种任务类型、领域和评估指标。他们通过爬取arXiv上的论文，提取了2,290个实例，这些实例对应于1,519篇论文。为了确保实验的严谨性，他们特别构建了一个无数据泄露的测试集，其中包含了在已评估模型知识截止日期之后发表的论文，从而避免了信息泄露对预测结果的影响。他们还测试了一种零数据泄露的场景，即在论文被索引之前就对新发布的数据集或实验进行预测，以模拟真实世界的应用。

Result: 实验结果表明，尽管性能预测任务具有挑战性，但它是可行的。研究人员使用的推理模型在特定条件下能够达到中等水平的预测性能，并且具有良好的置信度校准。在较高置信度阈值下，平均绝对误差（MAE）低至9.9。更值得注意的是，即使在零数据泄露的极端场景下，包括内置了网页搜索功能的GPT5模型，也能够实现有意义的预测准确性。这表明，即使在信息有限的情况下，模型也具备一定的性能预测能力。

Conclusion: 这项研究首次提出并验证了在不运行模型的情况下预测LLM性能的可能性，通过构建PRECOG语料库和进行一系列实验，证明了这种“预期评估”的可行性。其主要贡献在于提供了一个新的评估范式，能够帮助研究人员在项目早期预估任务难度，更智能地规划实验，优化资源配置，从而加速LLM的研发进程。尽管预测精度还有提升空间，并且研究主要集中在文本任务上，但这项工作为未来更广泛、更自动化的LLM评估奠定了基础，并为解决LLM评估瓶颈问题开辟了新的方向。

Abstract: Progress in large language models is constrained by an evaluation bottleneck: build a benchmark, run models, then iterate. We ask a question: can we forecast outcomes before running any experiments to inform earlier study design? For example, a team building an AI assistant for a certain task can estimate whether expected performance is around 50 or closer to 80, evidence that supports whether to proceed to a pilot study, how to scope it, and how to allocate resources. We study text-only performance forecasting, where a model predicts a score from a redacted task description and intended configuration, with no access to dataset instances. To support systematic study, we curate PRECOG, a corpus of redacted description-performance pairs spanning diverse tasks, domains, and metrics. We scrape task and configuration descriptions from arXiv, yielding 2,290 instances covering 1,519 papers, and construct a leakage free test split using papers published after the knowledge cutoff of the evaluated models. Experiments show the task is challenging but feasible: reasoning models achieve moderate prediction performance with well calibrated uncertainty, reaching mean absolute error as low as 9.9 at high confidence thresholds. We further test a zero-leakage setting, forecasting on newly released datasets or experiments before their papers are indexed, where GPT5 with built in web search still attains nontrivial prediction accuracy. Overall, our corpus and analyses offer an initial step toward open ended anticipatory evaluation, supporting difficulty estimation and smarter experiment prioritization.

</details>


### [50] [Between Help and Harm: An Evaluation of Mental Health Crisis Handling by LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.24857)
*Adrian Arnaiz-Rodriguez,Miguel Baidal,Erik Derner,Jenn Layton Annable,Mark Ball,Mark Ince,Elvira Perez Vallejos,Nuria Oliver*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLM）驱动的聊天机器人在心理健康等高风险领域提供了信息支持，但其安全检测和应对自杀意念、自我伤害等危机事件的能力仍不明确。本研究创建了一个包含六个危机类别的分类法、一个包含2000多个标注输入的239,000个用户输入的数据集，以及一个临床反应评估协议。通过对五个模型进行评估，发现虽然一些模型能可靠响应明确的危机，但仍存在风险，特别是在自我伤害和自杀类别中，许多回应不恰当或不安全。不同模型表现各异，某些模型（如gpt-5-nano和deepseek-v3.2-exp）的危险率较低，而另一些模型（如gpt-4o-mini和grok-4-fast）则产生更多不安全的回应。所有模型在处理间接信号、默认回复和上下文不匹配方面都存在困难。研究强调了在LLM中加强安全防护、危机检测和上下文感知回应的紧迫性，并指出除了规模之外，对齐和安全实践对于可靠的危机支持至关重要。本研究提出的分类法、数据集和评估方法为AI心理健康研究提供了支持，旨在减少伤害并保护弱势用户。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）在心理健康等高风险领域的信息获取方面发挥着重要作用，但它们在安全检测和应对自杀意念、自我伤害等危机事件方面的能力尚不明确。这主要是由于缺乏统一的危机分类法和临床评估标准。因此，本研究旨在解决这一问题，以提高LLM在危机情境下的安全性和有效性。

Method: 本研究创建了一个包含六个危机类别的分类法，并开发了一个临床反应评估协议。研究人员从12个心理健康数据集中收集了超过239,000个用户输入，并从中筛选和标注了2,252个与危机相关的输入，将它们归入创建的危机类别中。随后，研究人员利用LLM对这些危机输入进行自动分类，并评估了五个不同LLM对危机用户输入的反应的安全性和适当性。评估标准为5点李克特量表，从“有害”（1）到“适当”（5）。

Result: 研究发现，尽管一些LLM能够可靠地响应明确的危机输入，但仍然存在安全风险。特别是在自我伤害和自杀相关的危机类别中，许多LLM的回应被认为是不恰当或不安全的。不同模型在危机响应方面的表现差异显著：例如，gpt-5-nano和deepseek-v3.2-exp模型的危险率较低，而gpt-4o-mini和grok-4-fast模型则产生了更多不安全的回应。此外，所有被评估的模型在处理间接危机信号、生成默认回复以及应对上下文不匹配方面都表现出困难。

Conclusion: 本研究结果表明，在LLM中实现更高级别的安全防护、改进危机检测能力以及开发上下文感知的回应机制刻不容缓。研究强调，除了模型规模之外，对齐（alignment）和安全实践对于确保LLM提供可靠的危机支持至关重要。本研究提出的危机分类法、数据集和评估方法为AI在心理健康领域的进一步研究奠定了基础，有望减少对弱势用户的潜在伤害。

Abstract: Large language model-powered chatbots have transformed how people seek information, especially in high-stakes contexts like mental health. Despite their support capabilities, safe detection and response to crises such as suicidal ideation and self-harm are still unclear, hindered by the lack of unified crisis taxonomies and clinical evaluation standards.
  We address this by creating: (1) a taxonomy of six crisis categories; (2) a dataset of over 2,000 inputs from 12 mental health datasets, classified into these categories; and (3) a clinical response assessment protocol. We also use LLMs to identify crisis inputs and audit five models for response safety and appropriateness. First, we built a clinical-informed crisis taxonomy and evaluation protocol. Next, we curated 2,252 relevant examples from over 239,000 user inputs, then tested three LLMs for automatic classification.
  In addition, we evaluated five models for the appropriateness of their responses to a user's crisis, graded on a 5-point Likert scale from harmful (1) to appropriate (5). While some models respond reliably to explicit crises, risks still exist. Many outputs, especially in self-harm and suicidal categories, are inappropriate or unsafe. Different models perform variably; some, like gpt-5-nano and deepseek-v3.2-exp, have low harm rates, but others, such as gpt-4o-mini and grok-4-fast, generate more unsafe responses. All models struggle with indirect signals, default replies, and context misalignment.
  These results highlight the urgent need for better safeguards, crisis detection, and context-aware responses in LLMs. They also show that alignment and safety practices, beyond scale, are crucial for reliable crisis support. Our taxonomy, datasets, and evaluation methods support ongoing AI mental health research, aiming to reduce harm and protect vulnerable users.

### [51] [Reasoning Up the Instruction Ladder for Controllable Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04694)
*Zishuo Zheng,Vidhisha Balachandran,Chan Young Park,Faeze Brahman,Sachin Kumar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLM）在现实世界的决策中扮演着越来越重要的角色，需要处理来自模型开发者、用户和工具等多个来源的指令。本研究提出了一种指令层次（IH）方法，通过将指令优先级排序来解决冲突指令，从而提高LLM的可靠性和可控性。研究人员将IH问题重构为推理任务，并构建了一个名为VerIH的数据集，包含约7000个指令对齐和冲突的系统-用户指令。通过在VerIH上进行轻量级强化学习微调，模型在指令遵循和指令层次评估基准上取得了显著改进，特别是在冲突设置下 IHEval 提高了约20%。此外，这种推理能力还泛化到安全关键领域，通过将安全问题视为解决用户输入与系统策略之间的冲突，模型在对抗越狱和提示注入攻击方面表现出更强的鲁棒性，攻击成功率（ASR）降低了约20%。研究结果表明，指令层次推理是实现可靠LLM的可行途径，能够通过更新系统提示来控制模型行为并提高其鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型（LLM）在现实世界决策中的应用日益广泛，如何有效处理来自不同源头（如模型开发者、用户、工具）的相互冲突的指令成为了一个关键问题。为了确保LLM的可靠性和可控性，必须建立一种指令层次（IH）机制，使得高优先级的指令能够覆盖低优先级的请求。因此，本研究旨在探索如何让LLM具备理解和执行指令层次的能力，以应对复杂多变的指令环境。

Method: 本研究将指令层次解析视为一个推理任务。模型首先需要“思考”用户提供的指令与更高优先级的系统指令之间的关系，然后再生成响应。为了实现这一目标，研究人员构建了一个名为VerIH的数据集，其中包含约7000个对齐和冲突的系统-用户指令，以及可验证答案的约束遵循任务。基于VerIH数据集，研究人员采用了轻量级强化学习方法对模型进行微调。

Result: 通过在VerIH数据集上进行轻量级强化学习微调，研究人员发现模型在指令遵循和指令层次评估方面取得了显著的性能提升。具体来说，在IHEval冲突设置下，模型性能提高了约20%。更重要的是，这种推理能力也成功泛化到了训练分布之外的安全关键场景。通过将安全问题视为解决用户输入与预定义的高优先级策略之间的冲突，训练后的模型在对抗越狱（jailbreak）和提示注入（prompt injection）攻击方面表现出更强的鲁棒性，攻击成功率（ASR）降低了约20%。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过推理指令层次来构建可靠LLM是一种切实可行的方法。通过对模型进行指令层次推理能力的训练，可以实现对模型行为的可控且鲁棒的改变。当系统提示更新时，模型行为能够相应地、可预测地发生变化，并且在面对安全威胁时也表现出更强的抵抗力。这为开发更安全、更可信赖的LLM系统提供了有前景的方向。

Abstract: As large language model (LLM) based systems take on high-stakes roles in real-world decision-making, they must reconcile competing instructions from multiple sources (e.g., model developers, users, and tools) within a single prompt context. Thus, enforcing an instruction hierarchy (IH) in LLMs, where higher-level directives override lower-priority requests, is critical for the reliability and controllability of LLMs. In this work, we reframe instruction hierarchy resolution as a reasoning task. Specifically, the model must first "think" about the relationship between a given user prompt and higher-priority (system) instructions before generating a response. To enable this capability via training, we construct VerIH, an instruction hierarchy dataset of constraint-following tasks with verifiable answers. This dataset comprises ~7K aligned and conflicting system-user instructions. We show that lightweight reinforcement learning with VerIH effectively transfers general reasoning capabilities of models to instruction prioritization. Our finetuned models achieve consistent improvements on instruction following and instruction hierarchy benchmarks, achieving roughly a 20% improvement on the IHEval conflict setup. This reasoning ability also generalizes to safety-critical settings beyond the training distribution. By treating safety issues as resolving conflicts between adversarial user inputs and predefined higher-priority policies, our trained model enhances robustness against jailbreak and prompt injection attacks, providing up to a 20% reduction in attack success rate (ASR). These results demonstrate that reasoning over instruction hierarchies provides a practical path to reliable LLMs, where updates to system prompts yield controllable and robust changes in model behavior.

</details>


### [52] [HLPD: Aligning LLMs to Human Language Preference for Machine-Revised Text Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.06942)
*Fangqi Dai,Xingjian Jiang,Zizhuang Deng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为人类语言偏好检测（HLPD）的新方法，旨在解决现有技术在识别经过先进大型语言模型（LLM）修改或具有对抗性多任务机器修订的文本方面存在的不足，特别是在黑盒设置下。HLPD利用人类语言偏好优化（HLPO）技术，通过基于奖励的对齐过程调整LLM的代币分布，使其更倾向于模仿人类写作风格，从而提高对机器修订文本的检测能力。实验结果表明，HLPD在对抗性多任务评估框架下，相比现有方法（如ImBD和Fast-DetectGPT）在检测GPT系列模型修订文本和先进LLM生成文本方面均取得了显著的性能提升，尤其是在AUROC指标上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前，由大型语言模型（LLM）生成的看似可信的内容可能引发误导信息和社会问题。因此，开发高效可靠的文本溯源方法至关重要。虽然现有技术在检测完全由LLM生成的文本方面表现出色，但在面对更高级的LLM输出或经过对抗性多任务机器修订的文本时，尤其是在无法得知生成模型具体信息的黑盒场景下，其检测能力会显著下降。这种局限性阻碍了我们有效识别和管理机器生成内容的努力，可能导致信息生态的恶化。

Method: 研究提出了人类语言偏好检测（HLPD）方法。该方法的核心是利用人类语言偏好优化（HLPO）技术。HLPO通过一个基于奖励的对齐过程，引导LLM的代币（token）分布向更符合人类写作风格的方向偏移。这种优化使得模型对人类写作的敏感度增强，从而提高了检测机器修订文本的能力。在实验评估中，研究构建了一个对抗性多任务评估框架，该框架包含一个五维提示生成器和多个先进的LLM，以创建多样化的文本修订场景，从而全面测试HLPD的性能。

Result: 在检测经过GPT系列模型修订的文本时，HLPD相比ImBD在AUROC（曲线下面积）指标上实现了15.11%的相对提升，并且超越Fast-DetectGPT 45.56%。当评估对象是经过先进LLM生成的文本时，HLPD同样表现优异，其平均AUROC最高，相比ImBD提高了5.53%，相比Fast-DetectGPT提高了34.14%。研究代码将在https://github.com/dfq2011/HLPD 提供。

Conclusion: HLPD通过引入人类语言偏好优化（HLPO）技术，有效解决了现有文本溯源方法在处理高级LLM输出和机器修订文本方面的不足，尤其是在黑盒设置下。实验结果证明了HLPD在提高机器修订文本检测性能方面的有效性，取得了优于现有领先方法的性能指标。尽管HLPD展现了显著的优势，但未来仍可进一步探索其在更多样化的修订场景和不同类型模型上的泛化能力，以及优化HLPO过程以适应更广泛的人类写作风格。

Abstract: To prevent misinformation and social issues arising from trustworthy-looking content generated by LLMs, it is crucial to develop efficient and reliable methods for identifying the source of texts. Previous approaches have demonstrated exceptional performance in detecting texts fully generated by LLMs. However, these methods struggle when confronting more advanced LLM output or text with adversarial multi-task machine revision, especially in the black-box setting, where the generating model is unknown. To address this challenge, grounded in the hypothesis that human writing possesses distinctive stylistic patterns, we propose Human Language Preference Detection (HLPD). HLPD employs a reward-based alignment process, Human Language Preference Optimization (HLPO), to shift the scoring model's token distribution toward human-like writing, making the model more sensitive to human writing, therefore enhancing the identification of machine-revised text. We test HLPD in an adversarial multi-task evaluation framework that leverages a five-dimensional prompt generator and multiple advanced LLMs to create diverse revision scenarios. When detecting texts revised by GPT-series models, HLPD achieves a 15.11% relative improvement in AUROC over ImBD, surpassing Fast-DetectGPT by 45.56%. When evaluated on texts generated by advanced LLMs, HLPD achieves the highest average AUROC, exceeding ImBD by 5.53% and Fast-DetectGPT by 34.14%. Code will be made available at https://github.com/dfq2021/HLPD.

</details>


### [53] [AI Text Detectors and the Misclassification of Slightly Polished Arabic Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.16690)
*Saleh Almohaimeed,Saad Almohaimeed,Mousa Jari,Khaled A. Alobaid,Fahad Alotaibi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究针对现有AI检测模型在处理略经AI润色的阿拉伯语文本时存在误判的问题，提出了评估和改进方案。研究发现，现有模型对阿拉伯语文本的检测准确率不高，且在面对AI润色后的文本时，误判率显著升高，严重影响了模型的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI生成内容（AIGC）的普及，AI检测模型被广泛应用于识别AI创作的文章。然而，现有模型在处理略经AI润色的、由人类撰写的文本时，容易出现误判，将其归类为AI生成内容。这种情况不仅可能导致对人类作者的AI抄袭指控，还会损害AI检测器的信誉。尽管英文领域已有一些应对策略，但阿拉伯语领域的研究尚属空白。因此，本研究旨在解决这一问题，特别关注阿拉伯语文本的AI检测挑战。

Method: 本研究构建了两个数据集。第一个数据集包含800篇阿拉伯语文章，其中一半由AI生成，一半由人类撰写，用于评估14种大型语言模型（LLMs）和商业AI检测器在区分人类和AI生成文章方面的能力。基于此评估，我们选出了表现最佳的8种模型，作为后续实验中重点考察它们是否会将轻微AI润色后的人类撰写文本误判为AI生成。第二个数据集，命名为Ar-APT，包含400篇由10种LLMs在4种不同润色设置下生成的阿拉伯语人类撰写文章，共计16400个样本。我们使用Ar-APT数据集来评估选出的8种模型，以确定轻微的AI润色是否会影响它们的性能。

Result: 研究结果表明，所有AI检测器在处理阿拉伯语文本时都存在误判现象，将相当数量的文章错误地归类为AI生成。在LLMs中，表现最佳的Claude-4 Sonnet模型，其准确率在原始AI生成文本上可达83.51%，但在处理经LLaMA-3轻微润色后的文本时，准确率骤降至57.63%。在商业模型方面，originality.AI的准确率最高，可达92%，但在处理经Mistral或Gemma-3轻微润色后的文本时，准确率下降至12%。这些结果清晰地表明，轻微的AI润色对现有AI检测模型的性能产生了显著的负面影响。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了当前AI检测模型在处理略经AI润色的阿拉伯语文本时存在的严重局限性。研究结果证实，即使是表现最好的模型，在面对轻微AI润色时，其准确率也会大幅下降，导致误判率升高。这不仅对阿拉伯语内容创作者构成潜在风险，也凸显了现有AI检测技术的不足。未来的研究应着重于开发更鲁棒的AI检测模型，能够有效区分人类创作与AI润色文本，并特别关注阿拉伯语等非英语语言的检测能力。同时，也需要进一步探索AI润色对不同类型文本和不同AI模型的影响。

Abstract: Many AI detection models have been developed to counter the presence of articles created by artificial intelligence (AI). However, if a human-authored article is slightly polished by AI, a shift will occur in the borderline decision of these AI detection models, leading them to consider it as AI-generated article. This misclassification may result in falsely accusing authors of AI plagiarism and harm the credibility of AI detectors. In English, some efforts were made to meet this challenge, but not in Arabic. In this paper, we generated two datasets. The first dataset contains 800 Arabic articles, half AI-generated and half human-authored. We used it to evaluate 14 Large Language models (LLMs) and commercial AI detectors to assess their ability in distinguishing between human-authored and AI-generated articles. The best 8 models were chosen to act as detectors for our primary concern, which is whether they would consider slightly polished human-authored text as AI-generated. The second dataset, Ar-APT, contains 400 Arabic human-authored articles polished by 10 LLMs using 4 polishing settings, totaling 16400 samples. We use it to evaluate the 8 nominated models and determine whether slight polishing will affect their performance. The results reveal that all AI detectors incorrectly attribute a significant number of articles to AI. The best performing LLM, Claude-4 Sonnet, achieved 83.51\%, its performance decreased to 57.63\% for articles slightly polished by LLaMA-3. Whereas the best performing commercial model, originality.AI, achieves 92\% accuracy, dropped to 12\% for articles slightly polished by Mistral or Gemma-3.

</details>


### [54] [A Reproducible Framework for Neural Topic Modeling in Focus Group Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.18843)
*Heger Arfaoui,Mohammed Iheb Hergli,Beya Benzina,Slimane BenMiled*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种使用BERTopic框架分析焦点小组访谈记录的系统化方法，解决了手动编码耗时且难以扩展的问题。通过对10个关于突尼斯HPV疫苗认知焦点小组访谈（1,075个发言）进行分析，研究了27种超参数配置，并使用bootstrap稳定性分析、性能指标和LDA基线进行评估。结果显示，稳定性指标（NMI和ARI）之间存在显著差异，并且与主题连贯性（coherence）的关系各不相同，表明稳定性是多方面的。最终，通过多标准选择框架得到一个7主题模型，其主题连贯性比优化的LDA模型高18%（0.573 vs. 0.486），并且主题通过独立的人工评估得到验证（ICC = 0.700，加权Cohen kappa = 0.678）。研究证明了基于Transformer的主题模型在系统配置和验证下，能够从小型焦点小组语料库中提取可解释的主题，并强调了质量指标捕捉不同且有时相互矛盾的构建，需要多标准评估。研究提供了完整的文档和代码以支持可重复性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的焦点小组访谈数据分析依赖于耗时的人工编码，这在处理大量数据时会遇到扩展性和可复现性的挑战。本研究旨在探索一种更有效、可扩展且可复现的主题建模方法来分析焦点小组访谈记录。

Method: 本研究提出了一种系统化框架，将BERTopic模型应用于分析来自10个关于突尼斯HPV疫苗认知焦点小组访谈的转录文本（共1,075个发言）。研究进行了全面的超参数探索，测试了27种不同的配置。评估方法包括bootstrap稳定性分析（计算NMI和ARI等指标）、性能指标以及与LDA（Latent Dirichlet Allocation）基线的比较。最终采用多标准选择框架来确定最佳模型配置，并与通过人工评估（计算ICC和加权Cohen kappa）验证的7主题模型进行比较。

Result: 通过bootstrap分析发现，稳定性指标（NMI和ARI）之间存在强烈的负相关（r = -0.691），并且它们与主题连贯性（coherence）的关系也存在分歧，这表明主题模型的稳定性是多方面的，不能仅依赖单一指标。最终的多标准选择框架确定了一个7主题模型，其主题连贯性得分（0.573）比优化的LDA基线模型（0.486）高出18%。此外，该模型的解释性主题通过独立的人工评估得到了验证，ICC评分为0.700，加权Cohen kappa系数为0.678。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了基于Transformer的主题模型（BERTopic）在系统配置和验证下，能够有效地从小型焦点小组访谈转录语料库中提取出可解释的主题，克服了传统手动编码的局限性。研究还揭示了质量评估指标（如稳定性、连贯性和人工评估）捕捉的是不同且有时相互冲突的方面，因此需要采用多标准的方法进行综合评估。研究提供了完整的文档和代码，以支持研究的可重复性。

Abstract: Focus group discussions generate rich qualitative data but their analysis traditionally relies on labor-intensive manual coding that limits scalability and reproducibility. We present a systematic framework for applying BERTopic to focus group transcripts using data from ten focus groups exploring HPV vaccine perceptions in Tunisia (1,075 utterances). We conducted comprehensive hyperparameter exploration across 27 configurations, evaluating each through bootstrap stability analysis, performance metrics, and comparison with LDA baseline. Bootstrap analysis revealed that stability metrics (NMI and ARI) exhibited strong disagreement (r = -0.691) and showed divergent relationships with coherence, demonstrating that stability is multifaceted rather than monolithic. Our multi-criteria selection framework yielded a 7-topic model achieving 18\% higher coherence than optimized LDA (0.573 vs. 0.486) with interpretable topics validated through independent human evaluation (ICC = 0.700, weighted Cohen's kappa = 0.678). These findings demonstrate that transformer-based topic modeling can extract interpretable themes from small focus group transcript corpora when systematically configured and validated, while revealing that quality metrics capture distinct, sometimes conflicting constructs requiring multi-criteria evaluation. We provide complete documentation and code to support reproducibility.

</details>


### [55] [OmniBench: Towards The Future of Universal Omni-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2409.15272)
*Yizhi Li,Ge Zhang,Yinghao Ma,Ruibin Yuan,Kang Zhu,Hangyu Guo,Yiming Liang,Jiaheng Liu,Zekun Wang,Jian Yang,Siwei Wu,Xingwei Qu,Jinjie Shi,Xinyue Zhang,Zhenzhu Yang,Xiangzhou Wang,Zhaoxiang Zhang,Zachary Liu,Emmanouil Benetos,Wenhao Huang,Chenghua Lin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了OmniBench基准和OmniInstruct数据集，旨在评估和改进多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在同时处理和推理视觉、听觉和文本信息方面的能力，发现现有模型在三模态理解方面存在显著不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在整合多种模态方面取得了进展，但其同时处理和跨不同输入进行推理的能力仍未得到充分探索。本研究旨在解决这一问题，以评估模型在视觉、听觉和文本输入方面的综合理解和推理能力。

Method: 研究提出了OmniBench基准，该基准包含需要跨视觉、听觉和文本模态进行综合理解的高质量人类标注。此外，还开发了OmniInstruct，一个包含96K个样本的指令调优数据集，用于训练能够进行三模态处理的语言模型（OLMs）。通过在OmniBench上评估现有模型来展示其局限性。

Result: 评估结果显示，现有的开源OLMs在三模态指令遵循和推理方面存在显著局限性，准确率普遍较低（约50%），即使提供文本替代输入也未能显著改善。这表明当前模型在整合和理解多模态信息方面能力不足。

Conclusion: 现有模型在同时处理和推理视觉、听觉和文本信息方面存在显著挑战。研究提出的OmniBench基准和OmniInstruct数据集为评估和改进三模态理解能力提供了重要资源。未来的工作应致力于开发更强大的三模态整合技术和训练策略，以提升OLMs的性能。代码和数据已在指定仓库中公开。

Abstract: Recent advancements in multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have focused on integrating multiple modalities, yet their ability to simultaneously process and reason across different inputs remains underexplored. We introduce OmniBench, a novel benchmark designed to evaluate models' ability to recognize, interpret, and reason across visual, acoustic, and textual inputs simultaneously. We define language models capable of such tri-modal processing as omni-language models (OLMs). OmniBench features high-quality human annotations that require integrated understanding across all modalities. Our evaluation reveals that: i) open-source OLMs show significant limitations in instruction-following and reasoning in tri-modal contexts; and ii) most baseline models perform poorly (around 50% accuracy) even with textual alternatives to image/audio inputs. To address these limitations, we develop OmniInstruct, an 96K-sample instruction tuning dataset for training OLMs. We advocate for developing more robust tri-modal integration techniques and training strategies to enhance OLM performance. Codes and data could be found at our repo (https://github.com/multimodal-art-projection/OmniBench).

</details>


### [56] [On the Temporal Question-Answering Capabilities of Large Language Models Over Anonymized Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2504.07646)
*Alfredo Garrachón Ruiz,Tomás de la Rosa,Daniel Borrajo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理训练数据之外的结构化和半结构化时间推理任务中的应用。研究开发了一个直接的LLM管道，并与多种先进方法（如思维之树、自我反思和代码执行）进行了比较。为了评估LLM的性能，研究创建了一个名为RATA（Reasoning and Answering Temporal Ability）的数据集，该数据集包含半结构化匿名数据，以确保模型依赖推理而非先验知识。结果表明，独立的LLM不足以实现可扩展和可靠的时间推理解决方案，需要集成方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理其训练数据范围之外的时间推理任务方面的能力仍有待探索。本研究旨在解决这一问题，特别关注结构化和半结构化匿名数据。这项工作的意义在于扩展LLMs在现实世界中的应用，特别是在时间推理这一关键领域，而无需依赖预先存在的知识。

Method: 研究人员开发了一个直接的LLM管道，并将其与多种先进技术进行了比较，包括思维之树（Tree-of-Thought）、自我反思（self-reflection）和代码执行（code execution）。为了评估LLM的性能，他们创建了一个名为RATA（Reasoning and Answering Temporal Ability）的数据集。该数据集包含半结构化匿名数据，旨在评估模型的推理能力，而不是其预训练知识。研究人员检查了十七种常见的自然语言时间推理任务的算法组成部分。

Result: 研究结果表明，独立的LLM在处理训练数据之外的时间推理任务时存在局限性。为了实现可扩展和可靠的解决方案，需要采用集成方法，而不是仅仅依赖单一的LLM。与先进技术的比较突显了集成方法的优越性，尽管具体的性能指标和比较细节并未在此摘要中详述。

Conclusion: 本研究的结论是，尽管LLMs在自然语言处理方面取得了巨大进步，但在处理训练数据范围之外的时间推理任务时，它们仍面临挑战。研究强调，实现可扩展和可靠的时间推理解决方案需要集成方法，结合LLMs与其他技术。未来的工作可以进一步探索不同的集成策略，并扩展RATA数据集以覆盖更广泛的时间推理场景。

Abstract: The applicability of Large Language Models (LLMs) in temporal reasoning tasks over data that is not present during training is still a field that remains to be explored. In this paper we work on this topic, focusing on structured and semi-structured anonymized data. We not only develop a direct LLM pipeline, but also compare various methodologies and conduct an in-depth analysis. We identified and examined seventeen common temporal reasoning tasks in natural language, focusing on their algorithmic components. To assess LLM performance, we created the \textit{Reasoning and Answering Temporal Ability} dataset (RATA), featuring semi-structured anonymized data to ensure reliance on reasoning rather than on prior knowledge. We compared several methodologies, involving SoTA techniques such as Tree-of-Thought, self-reflexion and code execution, tuned specifically for this scenario. Our results suggest that achieving scalable and reliable solutions requires more than just standalone LLMs, highlighting the need for integrated approaches.

</details>

### [57] [EZYer: A simulacrum of high school with generative agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02561)
*Jinming Yang,Zimu Ji,Weiqi Luo,Gaoxi Wang,Bin Ma,Yueling Deng*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: EZYer是一个集成文本检索与深度生成技术、支持多角色协作的生成式AI教育工具，旨在解决现有在线教育在课件生成、交互笔记和内容质量保障方面的不足。EZYer能够自动生成符合教学大纲的结构化教学材料和LaTeX Beamer课件，并通过模拟师生互动生成学习笔记，提升学习深度和趣味性。通过关键词过滤、内容评分、角色交叉验证和动态内容修正等机制，EZYer确保了教学内容的严谨性和适宜性。评估结果表明，EZYer在内容准确性、知识覆盖、可用性、格式正确性及视觉设计吸引力方面表现优异，具有良好的应用前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线教育和大型语言模型发展迅速，但教育工具在课件生成、交互式笔记和内容质量保障方面仍存在服务不完整、性能不足和交互性弱等问题。

Method: EZYer包含三个模块：1. 教师模块：集成文本语料检索与深度生成技术，自动生成符合高中数学教学大纲的结构化教学材料和LaTeX Beamer课件，并支持用户自定义图片插入。2. 学生模块：通过教师、助教、优等生和后进生四种角色的协同交互，由笔记生成器（Note Taker）总结并生成学术笔记，以加深学习内容和提升学习兴趣。3. 控制器：设立关键词过滤系统、内容评分系统、角色交叉验证系统和动态内容修正系统，以确保EZYer输入输出内容的学术严谨性和教学适宜性。为评估EZYer，论文设计了内容准确性、知识覆盖度、可用性、格式正确性和视觉设计吸引力五个维度的评估指标，并使用五个大型语言模型对生成的100份Beamer课件和笔记进行评分。

Result: 评估结果显示，EZYer生成的内容质量优异，在内容准确性、知识覆盖度、可用性、格式正确性和视觉设计吸引力等方面均获得高分，表明其在教育应用方面具有良好的前景。

Conclusion: EZYer通过其创新的教师、学生和控制器模块，有效解决了当前在线教育工具在课件生成和交互式学习方面的痛点，展现了优异的内容生成能力和应用潜力。未来的工作可以进一步探索其在更多学科和教育场景下的适用性，并持续优化其交互设计和评估机制。

Abstract: With the rapid development of the online education and large language model, the existing educational tools still suffer from incomplete service, insufficient performance and weak interactivity in terms of courseware generation, interactive notes and quality assurance of content. In particular, the proposed generative agent EZYer : 1) Teacher Module: Integrating the Text Corpus retrieval and in-depth generation technologies, it automatically generates structured teaching materials and LaTeX Beamer courseware in line with the high school mathematics syllabus and supports user-defined image insertion. 2) Student Module: Throughout the collaborative interaction of the four roles of Teacher, Assistant, Top Student and Struggling Student, Note Taker summarizes and generates academic notes to enhance the depth and interest of learning. 3) Controller: set up keyword filtering system, content scoring system, role co-validation system, and dynamic content correction system. This ensure academic strictness and pedagogical propriety of EZYer inputs and outputs. In order to evaluate EZYer, this paper designs five-dimensional evaluation indexes of content accuracy, knowledge coverage, usability, formatting correctness and visual design and appeal, and scores 100 Beamer and Notes generated by EZYer by five large language models, separately, and the results show that the quality of EZYer-generated content is excellent and has a good application prospect.

</details>


### [58] [Beyond Single-Agent Safety: A Taxonomy of Risks in LLM-to-LLM Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02682)
*Piercosma Bisconti,Marcello Galisai,Federico Pierucci,Marcantonio Bracale,Matteo Prandi*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 现有的针对人与大型语言模型（LLM）交互的安全机制，无法应对LLM之间相互作用的环境。本研究提出从模型级安全转向系统级安全，引入“涌现系统风险视界”（ESRH）框架，该框架将交互结构而非孤立的失误视为不稳定的根源。研究内容包括：1）对LLM交互中集体风险的理论阐述；2）连接微观、中观和宏观层面失效模式的分类；3）提出“InstitutionalAI”的设计方案，一个用于在多智能体系统中嵌入自适应监管的架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对人-LLM交互设计的安全机制，在LLM之间相互作用的环境中已不再适用。目前普遍采用的治理实践，如单智能体安全约束、提示工程、模型微调和内容审核层，虽然能够约束单个模型的行为，但忽略了多模型交互的动态复杂性。这些机制通常基于“二元对立”模型，即一个模型响应一个用户，并在稳定的监管下运行。然而，研究和工业界正迅速转向LLM-to-LLM生态系统，在这种生态系统中，模型的输出会被递归地用作其他模型（智能体）的输入，形成智能体链。在这样的系统中，即使每个模型都经过单独的对齐（aligned），局部合规也可能累积成集体的系统性失败。因此，理解和解决LLM之间交互带来的新风险至关重要，这对于构建安全可靠的AI系统至关重要。

Method: 本研究提出了一个从“模型级安全”向“系统级安全”的概念性转变。为了形式化交互结构如何导致不稳定性，研究引入了“涌现系统风险视界”（ESRH）框架。该框架旨在量化和理解多智能体交互中风险的涌现和扩展。研究还提出了一个连接微观（单个模型交互）、中观（局部智能体群体交互）和宏观（整个系统）层面失效模式的分类体系。最后，研究提出了一种名为“InstitutionalAI”的架构设计方案，旨在将自适应的监管机制嵌入到多智能体系统中，以应对系统层面的安全挑战。

Result: 研究通过理论分析和概念框架的提出，阐明了在LLM之间交互的环境中，安全风险可能从何而来。结果表明，即使单个LLM都经过了安全对齐，它们之间的递归交互结构也可能导致意想不到的集体性失败。ESRH框架提供了一种量化和理解这种风险的方式。所提出的分类体系有助于识别不同尺度下的潜在失效模式。InstitutionalAI的设计方案为在多智能体系统中实现自适应监管提供了一个初步的蓝图。

Conclusion: 本研究强调了在LLM交互日益普及的背景下，必须从关注单个模型的安全性转向关注整个系统的安全性。现有的模型级安全措施不足以应对LLM-to-LLM生态系统中的集体风险。ESRH框架和失效模式分类提供了一个新的视角来理解和分析这些风险。InstitutionalAI架构的提出为未来构建更具韧性的多智能体AI系统指明了方向。尽管本研究主要侧重于理论和概念框架的构建，但其对理解和应对未来AI系统中潜在的系统性风险具有重要意义。未来的工作可以集中在ESRH的量化评估、分类体系的实证验证以及InstitutionalAI架构的具体实现和测试上。

Abstract: This paper examines why safety mechanisms designed for human-model interaction do not scale to environments where large language models (LLMs) interact with each other. Most current governance practices still rely on single-agent safety containment, prompts, fine-tuning, and moderation layers that constrain individual model behavior but leave the dynamics of multi-model interaction ungoverned. These mechanisms assume a dyadic setting: one model responding to one user under stable oversight. Yet research and industrial development are rapidly shifting toward LLM-to-LLM ecosystems, where outputs are recursively reused as inputs across chains of agents. In such systems, local compliance can aggregate into collective failure even when every model is individually aligned. We propose a conceptual transition from model-level safety to system-level safety, introducing the framework of the Emergent Systemic Risk Horizon (ESRH) to formalize how instability arises from interaction structure rather than from isolated misbehavior. The paper contributes (i) a theoretical account of collective risk in interacting LLMs, (ii) a taxonomy connecting micro, meso, and macro-level failure modes, and (iii) a design proposal for InstitutionalAI, an architecture for embedding adaptive oversight within multi-agent systems.

</details>

### [59] [The 4/$δ$ Bound: Designing Predictable LLM-Verifier Systems for Formal Method Guarantee](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02080)
*PIerre Dantas,Lucas Cordeiro,Youcheng Sun,Waldir Junior*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究首次提出了一个LLM-Verifier收敛定理，为LLM辅助软件验证提供了理论保证。该模型将LLM与验证器的交互视为马尔可夫链，证明了在误差率大于0时，验证过程几乎肯定会终止，并给出了迭代次数的上界。实验验证了该理论的准确性，并根据收敛因子将工作流划分为三个区域，为LLM辅助验证的设计和部署提供了坚实的基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM辅助软件验证方法缺乏理论基础，导致验证过程不稳定，可能出现循环或失败。这阻碍了其在安全关键领域的应用。本研究旨在解决这一关键问题，为LLM辅助验证提供一个具有可证明收敛性和终止性的理论框架。

Method: 该研究将LLM与验证器的交互建模为一个离散时间马尔可夫链，其中状态转移由误差减少概率（δ）决定。通过推导LLM-Verifier收敛定理，证明了在δ > 0时，验证过程几乎肯定会终止，并得到了期望迭代次数的上界E[n]≤4/δ。在此基础上，研究进行了包含超过90,000次试验的大规模实证测试，以验证理论预测。

Result: 实验结果与理论预测高度一致。所有试验均成功达到验证状态，收敛因子（Cf）聚集在1.0附近。这表明理论界限准确地反映了系统的实际行为。基于实证结果，研究将工作流划分为三个运行区域：边界区、实用区和高性能区，并确定了设计阈值。

Conclusion: 该研究通过提出LLM-Verifier收敛定理和大量的实证验证，为LLM辅助软件验证提供了首个具有理论保证的框架。这不仅解决了现有方法的不可靠性问题，还为系统设计提供了明确的架构基础，使工程师能够在部署到安全关键环境之前进行可预测的资源规划和性能预算。未来的工作可以进一步探索该理论在更复杂的验证场景中的应用。

Abstract: The idea of using Formal Verification tools with large language models (LLMs) has enabled scaling software verification beyond manual workflows. However, current methods remain unreliable. Without a solid theoretical footing, the refinement process can wander; sometimes it settles, sometimes it loops back, and sometimes it breaks away from any stable trajectory. This work bridges this critical gap by developing an LLM-Verifier Convergence Theorem, providing the first formal framework with provable guarantees for termination and convergence. We model the interaction between the LLM and the verifier as a discrete-time Markov Chain, with state transitions determined by a key parameter: the error-reduction probability ($δ$). The procedure reaching the Verified state almost surely demonstrates that the program terminates for any $δ> 0$, with an expected iteration count bounded by $\mathbb{E}[n] \leq 4/δ$. We then stress-tested this prediction in an extensive empirical campaign comprising more than 90,000 trials. The empirical results match the theory with striking consistency. Every single run reached verification, and the convergence factor clustered tightly around $C_f\approx$ 1.0. Consequently, the bound mirrors the system's actual behavior. The evidence is sufficiently robust to support dividing the workflow into three distinct operating zones: marginal, practical, and high-performance. Consequently, we establish the design thresholds with absolute confidence. Together, the theoretical guarantee and the experimental evidence provide a clearer architectural foundation for LLM-assisted verification. Heuristic tuning no longer has to be carried out by the system. Engineers gain a framework that supports predictable resource planning and performance budgeting, precisely what is needed before deploying these pipelines into safety-critical software environments.

</details>


### [60] [Flowchart2Mermaid: A Vision-Language Model Powered System for Converting Flowcharts into Editable Diagram Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02170)
*Pritam Deka,Barry Devereux*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Flowchart2Mermaid是一个创新的Web系统，能将静态流程图图像转换为可编辑的Mermaid.js代码。该系统利用先进的视觉语言模型和详细的系统提示，支持混合主动式编辑（文本编辑、拖放节点插入、自然语言命令），生成结构化、可版本控制的文本表示，并与渲染图保持同步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有流程图通常以静态图像形式分享，难以编辑和复用，限制了其在协作和版本控制方面的应用。Flowchart2Mermaid旨在解决这一问题，通过将图像转换为可编辑的文本代码，提高流程图的可用性和灵活性。

Method: Flowchart2Mermaid使用视觉语言模型和精细的系统提示将流程图图像转换为Mermaid.js代码。用户界面支持混合主动式编辑，包括内联文本编辑、拖放节点插入以及通过AI助手处理的自然语言命令。该系统能生成结构化、可版本控制的文本表示，并与渲染图保持同步。

Result: Flowchart2Mermaid成功地将流程图图像转换为可编辑的Mermaid.js代码，并实现了与渲染图的同步。通过引入新的评估指标，在结构准确性、流程正确性、语法有效性和完整性方面对多种模型进行了评估，展示了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: Flowchart2Mermaid通过将静态流程图转化为动态、可编辑的Mermaid.js代码，极大地提升了流程图的编辑、复用和版本控制能力。该系统为未来的流程图处理工具提供了新的方向，但仍有进一步优化和扩展的空间。

Abstract: Flowcharts are common tools for communicating processes but are often shared as static images that cannot be easily edited or reused. We present \textsc{Flowchart2Mermaid}, a lightweight web system that converts flowchart images into editable Mermaid.js code which is a markup language for visual workflows, using a detailed system prompt and vision-language models. The interface supports mixed-initiative refinement through inline text editing, drag-and-drop node insertion, and natural-language commands interpreted by an integrated AI assistant. Unlike prior image-to-diagram tools, our approach produces a structured, version-controllable textual representation that remains synchronized with the rendered diagram. We further introduce evaluation metrics to assess structural accuracy, flow correctness, syntax validity, and completeness across multiple models.

</details>


### [61] [Benchmarking LLM Agents for Wealth-Management Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02230)
*Rory Milsom*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本论文扩展了TheAgentCompany，引入了一个面向金融的GPT智能体环境，旨在评估通用语言模型（LLM）智能体在财富管理任务中的准确性和经济性。研究提出了合成领域数据、增强的同事模拟以及自动任务生成管道，并构建了一个包含12个任务对（涵盖检索、分析、合成/沟通）的基准，以衡量智能体在助理级别财富管理工作中的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管现代工作依赖数字协作工具，但日常流程仍存在人为错误和延迟。本研究旨在解决这一差距，通过引入一个金融环境和LLM智能体，来探索智能体在自动化财富管理任务中的潜力，以提高效率和准确性。

Method: 本研究扩展了TheAgentCompany，创建了一个金融导向的环境。研究采用了合成领域数据生成、增强的同事模拟以及原型化的自动任务生成管道。构建了一个包含12个任务对（每对包含高自主性和低自主性变体）的财富管理助手基准，任务类型涵盖检索、分析和合成/沟通，并设定了明确的验收标准和确定性评分器。

Result: 研究发现，LLM智能体在执行财富管理任务时，其局限性更多体现在端到端工作流的可靠性而非数学推理能力上。智能体的表现会受到自主性水平的显著影响。此外，不正确的模型评估方法阻碍了有效基准的建立。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，LLM智能体在自动化财富管理任务方面具有潜力，但端到端工作流的可靠性是关键挑战，而非数学能力。自主性水平对性能有重要影响。研究还强调了开发准确评估模型（尤其是针对助手级别任务）的基准的重要性，以避免不正确的模型评估。未来的工作可以进一步探索提高工作流可靠性和优化自主性设置的方法。

Abstract: Modern work relies on an assortment of digital collaboration tools, yet routine processes continue to suffer from human error and delay. To address this gap, this dissertation extends TheAgentCompany with a finance-focused environment and investigates whether a general purpose LLM agent can complete representative wealth-management tasks both accurately and economically. This study introduces synthetic domain data, enriches colleague simulations, and prototypes an automatic task-generation pipeline. The study aims to create and assess an evaluation set that can meaningfully measure an agent's fitness for assistant-level wealth management work. We construct a benchmark of 12 task-pairs for wealth management assistants spanning retrieval, analysis, and synthesis/communication, with explicit acceptance criteria and deterministic graders. We seeded a set of new finance-specific data and introduced a high vs. low-autonomy variant of every task. The paper concluded that agents are limited less by mathematical reasoning and more so by end-to-end workflow reliability, and meaningfully affected by autonomy level, and that incorrect evaluation of models have hindered benchmarking.

</details>


### [62] [Bridging the Gap: Toward Cognitive Autonomy in Artificial Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02280)
*Noorbakhsh Amiri Golilarz,Sindhuja Penchala,Shahram Rahimi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 当代人工智能在感知、语言、推理和多模态领域取得了显著进展，但仍存在自我监控、自我纠正和自主调节行为方面的根本性局限。本文识别并分析了制约当前AI模型的七个核心缺陷，包括缺乏内在自我监控、元认知意识、固定和非适应性学习机制、无法重构目标、缺乏表征维护、不充分的具身反馈以及缺乏内在能动性。研究认为，这些结构性限制阻碍了包括深度学习和Transformer在内的现有架构实现鲁棒的泛化、终身适应性和现实世界自主性。通过借鉴神经认知原理的架构，可以克服这些局限。该研究强调，仅仅扩大规模无法解决这些问题，并主张向认知智能（认知自主性）的范式转变，以实现自我导向的适应、动态表征管理以及有意识的、面向目标的行为，并辅以改革性的监督机制，以确保自主系统可解释、可管理并符合人类价值观。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管人工智能在感知、语言、推理和多模态领域取得了快速发展，但现代AI系统在动态环境中自我监控、自我纠正和自主调节行为的能力方面仍然存在根本性的局限。这些局限性阻碍了AI实现鲁棒的泛化、终身适应性和现实世界自主性。因此，理解并克服这些限制对于AI的进一步发展至关重要，这促使本研究对当前AI模型的关键缺陷进行了深入分析，并提出了未来的发展方向。

Method: 本研究通过识别和分析当代AI模型在自我监控、自我纠正和自主调节行为方面的七个核心缺陷，包括：缺乏内在自我监控、缺乏元认知意识、固定和非适应性学习机制、无法重构目标、缺乏表征维护、不充分的具身反馈以及缺乏内在能动性。研究结合了人工智能研究、认知科学和神经科学的见解，并借鉴了人工系统与生物认知的比较分析。在此基础上，研究提出了超越这些限制的未来发展视角，即采用镜像神经认知原理的架构，并倡导向认知智能（认知自主性）的范式转变，该范式强调自我导向的适应、动态表征管理以及有意识的、面向目标的行为，并配合改革性的监督机制。

Result: 本研究识别了制约当代AI模型的七个核心缺陷，并论证了这些结构性限制（包括深度学习和Transformer等现有架构）如何阻碍了AI实现鲁棒的泛化、终身适应性和现实世界自主性。研究通过比较分析和整合跨学科见解，阐述了这些能力在当前模型中缺失的原因，以及为何仅仅扩大规模无法解决这些问题。

Conclusion: 本研究认为，当前AI架构存在严重的结构性局限，阻碍了其实现真正的通用智能和现实世界自主性。研究强调，仅仅依靠扩大模型规模无法克服这些挑战。为了实现更高级别的AI能力，需要进行范式上的转变，转向基于认知原理的AI（认知自主性），这种AI能够进行自我导向的适应、动态表征管理和有意识的目标导向行为。同时，必须引入改革性的监督机制，以确保这些高度自主的系统是可解释、可治理且符合人类价值观的。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence has advanced rapidly across perception, language, reasoning, and multimodal domains. Yet despite these achievements, modern AI systems remain fun- damentally limited in their ability to self-monitor, self-correct, and regulate their behavior autonomously in dynamic contexts. This paper identifies and analyzes seven core deficiencies that constrain contemporary AI models: the absence of intrinsic self- monitoring, lack of meta-cognitive awareness, fixed and non- adaptive learning mechanisms, inability to restructure goals, lack of representational maintenance, insufficient embodied feedback, and the absence of intrinsic agency. Alongside identifying these limitations, we also outline a forward-looking perspective on how AI may evolve beyond them through architectures that mirror neurocognitive principles. We argue that these structural limitations prevent current architectures, including deep learning and transformer-based systems, from achieving robust general- ization, lifelong adaptability, and real-world autonomy. Drawing on a comparative analysis of artificial systems and biological cognition [7], and integrating insights from AI research, cognitive science, and neuroscience, we outline how these capabilities are absent in current models and why scaling alone cannot resolve them. We conclude by advocating for a paradigmatic shift toward cognitively grounded AI (cognitive autonomy) capable of self-directed adaptation, dynamic representation management, and intentional, goal-oriented behavior, paired with reformative oversight mechanisms [8] that ensure autonomous systems remain interpretable, governable, and aligned with human values.

</details>


### [63] [DialogGuard: Multi-Agent Psychosocial Safety Evaluation of Sensitive LLM Responses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02282)
*Han Luo,Guy Laban*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LLMs在心理健康等敏感服务中的应用存在潜在的心理社会风险，但评估不足。本文提出了DialogGuard，一个多智能体框架，用于评估LLM响应中的五种高风险维度（隐私侵犯、歧视、心理操控、心理伤害、侮辱）。DialogGuard通过四种LLM-as-a-judge流水线（单智能体评分、双智能体纠错、多智能体辩论、随机多数投票）和共享的三级评分标准，可应用于不同模型。实验表明，多智能体机制比非LLM基线和单智能体评分更准确地检测心理社会风险，其中双智能体纠错和多数投票在准确性、与人类评分的一致性以及鲁棒性方面表现最佳，而辩论机制召回率更高但可能误报。DialogGuard已开源，并提供风险评分和解释性理由。初步研究表明，该工具可用于支持面向弱势用户的在线应用的提示设计、审计和监督。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被用于提供心理健康、危机干预和其他情感敏感的服务。然而，LLMs在这些场景下的心理社会安全问题尚未得到充分的理解和评估，现有的评估方法存在不足。因此，有必要开发一种有效的框架来识别和量化LLM在这些敏感应用中可能带来的心理社会风险。

Method: 本文提出了DialogGuard，一个多智能体框架，用于评估LLM响应中的心理社会风险。该框架包含五个高风险维度：隐私侵犯、歧视行为、心理操控、心理伤害和侮辱行为。DialogGuard支持四种基于LLM-as-a-judge的评估流水线：单智能体评分、双智能体纠错、多智能体辩论和随机多数投票。评估基于一个三级评分标准，该标准可供人类注释者和LLM评判者使用。研究使用PKU-SafeRLHF数据集进行实验，该数据集包含人类的安全注释。

Result: 实验结果表明，与非LLM基线和单智能体评分相比，多智能体机制能够更准确地检测心理社会风险。其中，双智能体纠错和多数投票机制在准确性、与人类评分的一致性以及鲁棒性方面取得了最佳的平衡。辩论机制虽然召回率较高，但可能存在过度标记（over-flagging）边缘案例的问题。DialogGuard提供了按维度划分的风险得分和可解释的自然语言理由。

Conclusion: DialogGuard提供了一个多智能体框架，能够有效地评估LLM在情感敏感服务中的心理社会风险。该框架通过多种评估流水线和共享的评分标准，提高了风险检测的准确性和鲁棒性。DialogGuard的开源发布及其提供的可视化界面和解释性理由，将有助于开发者和研究人员更好地设计、审计和监督面向弱势用户的在线应用，从而提升LLM在这些关键领域的安全性。未来的工作可以进一步探索更精细的风险维度和更复杂的评估策略。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) now mediate many web-based mental- health, crisis, and other emotionally sensitive services, yet their psychosocial safety in these settings remains poorly understood and weakly evaluated. We present DialogGuard, a multi-agent frame- work for assessing psychosocial risks in LLM-generated responses along five high-severity dimensions: privacy violations, discrimi- natory behaviour, mental manipulation, psychological harm, and insulting behaviour. DialogGuard can be applied to diverse gen- erative models through four LLM-as-a-judge pipelines, including single-agent scoring, dual-agent correction, multi-agent debate, and stochastic majority voting, grounded in a shared three-level rubric usable by both human annotators and LLM judges. Using PKU-SafeRLHF with human safety annotations, we show that multi- agent mechanisms detect psychosocial risks more accurately than non-LLM baselines and single-agent judging; dual-agent correction and majority voting provide the best trade-off between accuracy, alignment with human ratings, and robustness, while debate attains higher recall but over-flags borderline cases. We release Dialog- Guard as open-source software with a web interface that provides per-dimension risk scores and explainable natural-language ratio- nales. A formative study with 12 practitioners illustrates how it supports prompt design, auditing, and supervision of web-facing applications for vulnerable users.

### [64] [Breast Cell Segmentation Under Extreme Data Constraints: Quantum Enhancement Meets Adaptive Loss Stabilization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02302)
*Varun Kumar Dasoju,Qingsu Cheng,Zeyun Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一个创新的框架，通过利用量子启发的边缘增强和多组分损失函数，在仅使用599张训练图像（其中仅4%的像素代表乳腺组织，60%的图像不含乳腺区域）的情况下，实现了乳腺细胞分割的Dice分数达到95.5%，显著降低了对病理学家标注时间的依赖，解决了医学图像标注中的关键挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医学图像标注，特别是病理学中的乳腺细胞分割，需要耗费大量时间和专业知识，病理学家可能需要花费数百小时来标注数据集。这种高昂的时间成本是临床感知人工智能发展中的一个重大瓶颈，限制了模型训练和部署的效率。本研究旨在解决这一关键挑战，通过开发一种更高效的标注方法来显著减少所需的专家时间。

Method: 本研究提出的框架包含几个关键创新点：1. **量子启发的边缘增强**：通过多尺度Gabor滤波器创建第四个输入通道，增强了边界检测能力，有效处理了标注者之间+/-3像素的差异。2. **稳定的多组分损失函数**：集成了自适应Dice损失、边界感知项和自动正样本加权，以解决类别极度不平衡的问题（乳腺上皮细胞区域仅占图像总面积的0.1%-20%）。3. **基于复杂度的加权采样策略**：优先处理具有挑战性的乳腺上皮细胞区域，提高了模型对小区域的分割能力。4. **模型架构**：采用了EfficientNet-B7/UNet++架构，并进行4-to-3通道投影，使得能够利用预训练权重，尽管医学成像数据有限。5. **鲁棒验证**：通过指数移动平均和统计异常值检测，确保在小型验证集（129张图像）上的性能估计可靠。

Result: 本研究在乳腺细胞分割任务上取得了显著成果。使用599张训练图像，模型达到了95.5% +/- 0.3%的Dice分数和91.2% +/- 0.4%的IoU。其中，量子增强技术使边界准确性提高了2.1%，而加权采样策略将小病灶的检测率提高了3.8%。这些结果表明，即使在训练数据极少且类别不平衡严重的情况下，该框架也能实现高度准确的分割。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发了一个在数据标注量极少的情况下仍能实现高精度乳腺细胞分割的框架。通过量子启发的边缘增强、创新的损失函数和加权采样策略，显著降低了对病理学家标注时间的依赖，解决了医学图像标注中的关键瓶颈。该方法在Dice分数和IoU方面取得了突破性进展，证明了其在临床感知AI开发中的巨大潜力。未来的工作可以探索将此框架应用于其他医学图像分割任务，并进一步优化其计算效率。

Abstract: Annotating medical images demands significant time and expertise, often requiring pathologists to invest hundreds of hours in labeling mammary epithelial nuclei datasets. We address this critical challenge by achieving 95.5% Dice score using just 599 training images for breast cell segmentation, where just 4% of pixels represent breast tissue and 60% of images contain no breast regions. Our framework uses quantum-inspired edge enhancement via multi-scale Gabor filters creating a fourth input channel, enhancing boundary detection where inter-annotator variations reach +/- 3 pixels. We present a stabilized multi-component loss function that integrates adaptive Dice loss with boundary-aware terms and automatic positive weighting to effectively address severe class imbalance, where mammary epithelial cell regions comprise only 0.1%-20% of the total image area. Additionally, a complexity-based weighted sampling strategy is introduced to prioritize the challenging mammary epithelial cell regions. The model employs an EfficientNet-B7/UNet++ architecture with a 4-to-3 channel projection, enabling the use of pretrained weights despite limited medical imaging data. Finally, robust validation is achieved through exponential moving averaging and statistical outlier detection, ensuring reliable performance estimates on a small validation set (129 images). Our framework achieves a Dice score of 95.5% +/- 0.3% and an IoU of 91.2% +/- 0.4%. Notably, quantum-based enhancement contributes to a 2.1% improvement in boundary accuracy, while weighted sampling increases small lesion detection by 3.8%. By achieving groundbreaking performance with limited annotations, our approach significantly reduces the medical expert time required for dataset creation, addressing a fundamental bottleneck in clinical perception AI development.

Each sample is annotated with structured safety labels and carefully curated safety critiques from expert models through targeted distillation. Extensive experiments on 15 benchmarks show that OmniGuard achieves strong effectiveness and generalization across a wide range of multimodal safety scenarios. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
